<div id="review_1427709884" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1427709884" />
    <a title="Redfox5" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/3816075-redfox5"><img alt="Redfox5" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1512680087p2/3816075.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1427709884?book_show_action=true">Oct 28, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Redfox5" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Redfox5" href="/user/show/3816075-redfox5">Redfox5</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3816075-redfox5?shelf=zombie">zombie</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3816075-redfox5?shelf=horror">horror</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3816075-redfox5?shelf=graphic-novel">graphic-novel</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3816075-redfox5?shelf=fiction">fiction</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3816075-redfox5?shelf=comics">comics</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3816075-redfox5?shelf=usa">usa</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1427709884" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer13764324169635689172"> Like most people, I was introduced to The Walking Dead through the TV Show. I'm a massive zombie fan. I have no problem watching the cheesiest zombie films going. And I have my 'end of the world' plan in place. So it was great to have a awesome TV show to watch. <br/><br/> I fell in love with The Walking Dead instantly. Season one and two were amazing but after that the love started to sour slightly. I'm a binge watcher, I wait till everything is on boxset then go for it. But I started watching season 3,</span>
  <span id="freeText13764324169635689172" style="display:none"> Like most people, I was introduced to The Walking Dead through the TV Show. I'm a massive zombie fan. I have no problem watching the cheesiest zombie films going. And I have my 'end of the world' plan in place. So it was great to have a awesome TV show to watch. <br /><br /> I fell in love with The Walking Dead instantly. Season one and two were amazing but after that the love started to sour slightly. I'm a binge watcher, I wait till everything is on boxset then go for it. But I started watching season 3, week by week and all the flaws stood out by a mile. I actually thought about giving up but then I brought the boxset, binged again and loved it. But the thing I really dislike about the show is the Characters. I hate the characters, they are so stupid and the fact that any of them have still managed to stay alive is beyond me. There are exceptions obviously, Michonne, Daryl and Glen. <br /><br /> I was really interested to see what these characters would be like in their original forms. Looks wise, none of them look like their TV counterparts but I find them all less annoying. And I haven't wished for Andrea dead once. It's hard to get over some of the relationships though, Andrea and Dale....ewww. <br /><br /> Story wise it's great. Most of it is recognisable from the show but there is enough differences to keep it interesting. I can understand why things were changed.<br /><br /> I'm not a massive fan of the artwork, some of the faces are odd. And the kids look really creepy. The zombies look good though and the artwork in colour at the back is stunning.<br /><br /> Would highly recommend this to fans of the show or zombie fans in general and I can't wait to read the rest! </span>
  <a data-text-id="13764324169635689172" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('L1B5bewG8ylvZuwn07vVoTjS2dX7obW8VVn6bN+zFtLM3IMRCFOHWt2G980Ut2G7/SEiaQ2w4DiRvEM+ZWGpRQ==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('IDzGl3xETD5yzp4g1CK8s63F1EOSLrIFpfNTQMrGM6XDsDzrmBE4TcAuhcoTLgipaDYv/2Q/54FhFuoScBSMMg==')})
  }
//]]>

      <div id="aboutAuthor" class=" clearFloats bigBox"><div class="h2Container gradientHeaderContainer"><h2 class="brownBackground"><a href="/author/show/12425.Robert_Kirkman">About Robert Kirkman</a></h2></div><div class="bigBoxBody"><div class="bigBoxContent containerWithHeaderContent">
          <div class='bookAuthorProfile'>
<div class='bookAuthorProfile__topContainer'>
<div class='bookAuthorProfile__photoContainer'>

</a></div>

<div class='bookAuthorProfile__about'>

<span id="freeTextContainer4236267498429535758">Robert Kirkman is an American comic book writer best known for his work on The Walking Dead, Invincible for Image Comics, as well as Ultimate X-Men and Marvel Zombies for Marvel Comics. He has also collaborated with Image Comics co-founder Todd McFarlane on the series Haunt. He is one of the five partners of Image Comics, and the only one of the five who was not one of the original co-founders of </span>
  <span id="freeText4236267498429535758" style="display:none">Robert Kirkman is an American comic book writer best known for his work on The Walking Dead, Invincible for Image Comics, as well as Ultimate X-Men and Marvel Zombies for Marvel Comics. He has also collaborated with Image Comics co-founder Todd McFarlane on the series Haunt. He is one of the five partners of Image Comics, and the only one of the five who was not one of the original co-founders of that publisher.<br /><br />Robert Kirkman's first comic books were self-published under his own Funk-o-Tron label. Along with childhood friend Tony Moore, Kirkman created Battle Pope which was published in late 2001. Battle Pope ran for over 2 years along with other Funk-o-Tron published books such as InkPunks and Double Take. <br /><br />In July of 2002, Robert's first work for another company began, with a 4-part SuperPatriot series for Image, along with Battle Pope backup story artist Cory Walker. Robert's creator-owned projects followed shortly thereafter, including Tech Jacket, Invincible and Walking Dead.</span>
  <a data-text-id="4236267498429535758" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

</div>
